  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_3d175558-a707-4917-8913-134fcd38dc74'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

<div id="review_1314927783" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1314927783" />
    <a title="Jules" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31272450-jules"><img alt="Jules" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1404792768p2/31272450.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1314927783?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jules" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jules" href="/user/show/31272450-jules">Jules</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31272450-jules?shelf=bdsm">bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31272450-jules?shelf=my-reviews">my-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31272450-jules?shelf=authors-b">authors-b</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1314927783" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12069775621207413680">Considering how much I loved <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23251003.Dom_Wars_Rounds_1__2__3__Dom_Wars___1_3_' title='Dom Wars Rounds 1, 2, 3 (Dom Wars, #1-3) by Lucian Bane' rel='nofollow noopener'>Dom Wars: Rounds 1, 2, 3</a>, this book really surprised me. Parts 1-3 were really hot, had lots of good chemistry between the characters, and the plot was pretty good. Parts 4-6 absolutely fell flat.<br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[The first thing that absolutely drove me nuts was the plot to #4. Tara isn't a stupid woman, and really, between her, Lucian and Steve, they couldn't come up with a way to get a hand on Lucian's text messages BEFORE the end of the round? If I were Lucian, I'd </span></span>
  <span id="freeText12069775621207413680" style="display:none">Considering how much I loved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23251003.Dom_Wars_Rounds_1__2__3__Dom_Wars___1_3_" title="Dom Wars Rounds 1, 2, 3 (Dom Wars, #1-3) by Lucian Bane" rel="nofollow noopener">Dom Wars: Rounds 1, 2, 3</a>, this book really surprised me. Parts 1-3 were really hot, had lots of good chemistry between the characters, and the plot was pretty good. Parts 4-6 absolutely fell flat.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The first thing that absolutely drove me nuts was the plot to #4. Tara isn't a stupid woman, and really, between her, Lucian and Steve, they couldn't come up with a way to get a hand on Lucian's text messages BEFORE the end of the round? If I were Lucian, I'd have gotten Steve to convince Tara to look at Lucian's sexts, problem solved, minimum drama. And the whole thing was just so weird...like trying to throw in obnoxious "50 Shades" bullshit and rationalizing the abuse as "part of the game".<br /><br /><br />And poor Steve. In the first four parts, we see Steve as a competent, former Secret Service agent who can get shit done. Suddenly, in 5 &amp; 6, Steve becomes a bumbling, stuttering Evangelical who can't even discuss sex without having to pray for his soul. It was so awkward I cringed. Incidentally, nonsensical personality changes in characters are a big pet peeve, and contributed to ruining the book.<br /><br />Then there was the character of Preacher. Was this supposed to be Christian BDSM fiction or not? If it was, that's fine, but start the theme in part 1, don't throw it in half way through part 5. It was added in almost like an afterthought, and not very well planned out. Preacher himself is a fascinating character who might be better off used for his own book instead of a secondary character in "Dom Wars" and as a half-formed plot-device. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Anyway, it wasn't BAD, but it could use a good polishing.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12069775621207413680" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Preacher will teach them all so much. This is a hard man, but find out what made him that way. The experience of book 5 (HILARIOUS BOOK!!!) will help keep them alive in book 6 where a mix of Survivor and Hunger Games comes into play...but with plenty of steamy sex. Lucian held nothing back when writing these books!</span>

<div id="review_1234840635" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1234840635" />
    <a title="Candy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34276124-candy"><img alt="Candy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586472066p2/34276124.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1234840635?book_show_action=true">Mar 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candy" href="/user/show/34276124-candy">Candy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1234840635" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9678961259724802101">Trust and faith was really put to the test during this 4th book in the series. It was interesting to find myself literally laughing during a couple of the smaller assignments, only to turn around and be completely irate on a few of them. I felt quite a bit of frustration for the two of them when I wasn't overly busy getting ready to kill.<br/>Lucian and Tara both have so much to overcome. She is dealing with him. He is dealing with his past and present. The assignments are being met with hesitation. </span>
  <span id="freeText9678961259724802101" style="display:none">Trust and faith was really put to the test during this 4th book in the series. It was interesting to find myself literally laughing during a couple of the smaller assignments, only to turn around and be completely irate on a few of them. I felt quite a bit of frustration for the two of them when I wasn't overly busy getting ready to kill.<br />Lucian and Tara both have so much to overcome. She is dealing with him. He is dealing with his past and present. The assignments are being met with hesitation. Tara is doing her best to be strong while Lucian tries his best not to just fall apart. They are both worried about what the future holds for them.<br /><br />Every time I read another book of the Dom Wars I am struck with surprise by the laughter that comes out of me. All of the odd things that come to light leave me laughing and anticipating the next moment. So, laughing in book 5? Not a huge surprise!<br />Because there was some cheating involved in the beginning of the forth book, Lucian, Tara, and Steve are required to obey Preacher, the top Dom from Africa during the fifth round. Lucian is very unhappy about the situation and worried for Tara and Steve because preacher doesn't look or act reasonable.<br />The three of them are required to sell unusual items in places that definitely doesn't need them. If denied a sale by a company they have to suffer the consequences. What is something that a toy store, an ob/gyn, and a funeral parlor don't need? You have to read it to find out! With preacher watching over them how much could possibly go wrong?<br /><br />I have really enjoyed the way everything unfolded throughout the 6th book. There wasn't a moment of laughter to be had for me. I became angry for the characters, I gagged during some of the things they had to deal with, and I never knew what was going to happen next.<br />This book wasn't one I could have guessed at. Things weren't bad, they were downright horrific! The only thing I knew for sure was that certain members would make it out alive because Mr. Bane has already started the WKDA series. I loved reading about the relationship between Tara and Lucian, but, I also enjoyed the other relationships they gained through being contestants on Dom Wars. Everybody served a purpose and their different personalities shined right through with the words used to explain. They all had individual strengths and weaknesses that were brought to the front, exposed to everyone else, and assistance given with teamwork.<br />Soon to read WKDA The Beginning...</span>
  <a data-text-id="9678961259724802101" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1187362681" />
    <a title="SB Morales" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21425975-sb-morales"><img alt="SB Morales" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1405270003p2/21425975.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1187362681?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="SB Morales" class="user" itemprop="url" name="SB Morales" href="/user/show/21425975-sb-morales">SB Morales</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1187362681" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16970429186749631720">Round 4<br/>It's time for Lucian Bane to face those demons. This time around we get to see the vulnerability that Lucian keeps well hidden. Most of the series Tara was the one who needed to be protected and Lucian needed to break through those walls. This time tho Tara is the one protecting Lucian. It was a great change to the protector turn into the protected. Tara does it with all she has. I am so excited to see Round 5 and find out where Bane takes us next.<br/><br/>Round 5<br/>This is my favorite installment of</span>
  <span id="freeText16970429186749631720" style="display:none">Round 4<br />It's time for Lucian Bane to face those demons. This time around we get to see the vulnerability that Lucian keeps well hidden. Most of the series Tara was the one who needed to be protected and Lucian needed to break through those walls. This time tho Tara is the one protecting Lucian. It was a great change to the protector turn into the protected. Tara does it with all she has. I am so excited to see Round 5 and find out where Bane takes us next.<br /><br />Round 5<br />This is my favorite installment of the series so far. I loved how the team of three works together not only just to complete there mission, but to be there to lean on each other. The Preacher was an amazing character! This round made me laugh, cry, swoon, and surprised me! I can't wait to find out what is in store for these characters in the next round!<br /><br />Round 6<br /><br />This is it Tara and Lucian go into the final round along with the Preacher. This round was heart pounding suspense from start to finish! Of course the erotic scenes are amazing. Bane's scenes always are! The bond that the foursome has created is just amazing to me. You have to be dominated in order to dominate. The foursome didn't just blindly follow the top dom. They trusted him, because he earned that trust. It takes a strong person to give up control. These couples aren't, what I consider a, Dom/Sub couple. They are each strong enough in themselves to be lead and strong enough to lead when they needed to. This was an amazing series of strength and love. I can't wait to follow these characters into the next series. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16970429186749631720" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

The final rounds of Dom Wars come to a close with in these works (though he continues Lucian and Tara's story past here) and its gripping and moving straight through the last '.'! I ha</span>
  <span id="freeText9651680024903247577" style="display:none"><strong>Amazing!!! Love, love, LOVE this author!!</strong><br /><br />Now let me say... Very few authors can write a work that has me turned on, laughing out loud, connecting with their characters on an emotional level, and able to FEEL for them as if I have become that person myself. But, that is what Lucian Bane has done with these books... The final rounds of Dom Wars come to a close with in these works (though he continues Lucian and Tara's story past here) and its gripping and moving straight through the last '.'! I have not read the next chapter of their lives but I most DEFINITELY will! Lucian's struggle with Faith and finding God while being a sexual Dom- what many Christians would consider impossible- has me enthralled and, for lack of a better word, HOOKED!! Don't bypass this series, my fellow readers... Otherwise you will be missing out on a TRUE art!</span>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('PjfhGsKumvpqxhdc/JzHTMrzhuwrmIyaUWpHTlqQNBd5eAzmK9BD4DWfW2LodgfY00AHWELhE5UelHagudye4g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NI22v9c9Z6qH45ecQdutND+VMVgPB4BrDOf8c9/3SYZzwltDPkO+sNi626JVMW2gJiaw7GZ+H2RDGc2dPLvjcw==')})
  }
//]]>
